Liaoning Urban Transport Project-Anshan Subproject     Environmental Imract Assessment
EXECUTIVE SUMMARY
I PROJECT DESCRIPTION
Jianguo Road Reconstruction (JRR) project is the Anshan subproject of Liaoning Urban
Transport Project using loan from the World Bank, which includes the following five
components:
A) Road Infrastructure
The project which shAli involve a road section of 18.87 km in total length, includes Jianguo
Road's (south-north) widening and extension to north; construction of Hebei Road to connect
the northern exit of the city; widening and reconstruction of Huangang Road (east-west) and
Yongchang Street (east-west); construction of Wuyi Road Interchange as main crossing at the
meeting point of Huangang Road with Yongchang Street; widening, reconstruction and
extension to south of Yuanlin Road and Zhonghua Road to connect South Ring Road which
will be extended to east; movement (required by widening of Jianguo Road) of tram line (now
located at Jianguo Road and its west side) to the west close to Zhongchang Railway.
Refer to Fig. 2-3 and Table 2-2 through 2-4 about the layout of road infrastructure.
B) Traffic Management
*  Building of three new social parking lots in Hunan, Zhanqian and the People's park area.
*  Channelization of eight intersections (Yuanlin Rd.. Sandaojie and Wuyi Rd. Intersections
etc.).
*  Furnish the traffic signs and markings.
*  Provide and renew the traffic light facilities (at Jianguo Rd., Huangang Rd., Yongchang
St. and South Ring Rd. etc.).
*  Provide the median separator. pedestrian physical separator and separation facilities
'separating the motor vehicle and non-motor vehicle on Jianguo Rd., Huangang Rd..
Yongchang Street, Shengli Road. Yuanlin Road. Jiefang Road.
*  Set up 4 non-motor vehicle lanes on Lishan Street. Youai Street etc..
C) Public Transport
*  Set up three bus special lanes (Shengli Road Center Bus Lane Project. Renmin Road
Bus/NMV Only Road. Zhonghua Road Tram/NMV Only Road).
* . Set up Wuyi Bus Transfer Station.
D) Road Maintenance
*  Reconstruct 4.0 km-long l-longqi Road (Enclosing wall of enterprises on the both sides of
this road will remain unchanged.
*  Pave 6 walkways for pedestrian (Shuguang Street etc.).



Liaoning Urban Transport Project-Anshan Subproject     Environmental Impact Assessment
E) Technical Assistance
It shall include the MVECS. other TA and training items.
Auxiliary items include traffic control, public transport and road maintenance etc.. For brief
introduction and distribution of auxiliary items, see Table 2-5 and Fig. 2-4. Implementation
of auxiliary items shall exert less influence on environment than construction of
infrastructure.
As a part of outer frarmne "'" (outer circle road ), the South Ring Road, West Ring Road and
North Ring Road wer6 principally implemented. The roads at four ends of "t" from "EP"
(east, south, west and north of the city ) were also finished (see Fig.2-2). The project mainly
concerns the "+" skeleton which is the key part for realization of Anshan Urban Traffic
Development Program.
The total investment of JRR project amounts to 1268.0622 million Yuan RMB among which
34.6297 million Yuan RMB is used for environment protection.
2 ENVIRONMENTAL SURVEY AND PRESENT
ENVIRONMENTAL CONDITIONS
Anshan city, located in the middle of Liaoning Province (see Fig. 1-1), is a heavily industrial
city. The plant area of Anshan Iron & Steel Complex (AISC, employees 0.2 million ) is
concentrated on the northwest to the city, occupying 1/4 land of the city. 0.2 million AISC's
employees going to and off work result in tidewise traffic. Present status of Anshan's road
traffic is as follows: sparse road network, low traffic capacity of roads, inconvenient traffic
r4om-east -to-west, more road break-off because of different land use of the city. For details,
see Fig. 2-1.
For this assessment, air quality and traffic noise have been monitored in summer and winter,
obtaining 8092 monitoring data of air quality and 1544 data of noise and vibration.
Monitoring results of routine measurement and this assessment show that the noise level on
the both sides of roads in urban area generally has exceeded the standard, especially at night
(max. excess 15.3 dB), air environmental quality is poor, the hourly concentration of all
pollution factors has exceeded the standard, the daily average values have exceeded the
standard, in which the excess rates of HC and B[a]P are 100%. For details, see Table 3-2,
Table 3-3, Table 3-5, Fig. 3-2 - 3-6. For survey of social environment, see Fig. 3-7 through 3-
9.
At present, the main problems that the city of Anshan faces are the traffic noise pollution and
air pollution resulting from the industrial pollinate, meanwhile, the traffic congestion cause
inconvenience to the outgoing of the public.
2



Liaoning Urban Transport Project-Anshan Subproject       Environmental Impact Assessment
3 ENVIRONMENTAL IMPACT
3.1 Comparison of With and Without JRR in 2010
The negative impact of traffic noise with JRR on the other roads within the urban area is
slightly lower than without JRR.
With JRR, the total emission of CO, NOx, NO2 and HC from vehicles in the whole city is less
23.36%, 17.86%, 17.86% and 21.72% respectively than that of without JRR.
The JRR project hag significant importance for inhibiting further deterioration of Anshan air
environment, but alsQ a little negative impact in the view of traffic noise and pedestrians
walking at some sections.
Moving of tram line will solve the problem of mutual interference of vehicles and tramcars.
The interference occurs mainly in front of Anshan Railway Station, at Jianguo Road section
from Rainbow Bridge to Wuyi Road Intersection and at area near Lishan Underpass. In the
meantime, the negative impact of tramcar noise on the residents along the line will be
reduced.
3.2 Positive Impact
Relieve traffic pressure of other trunk roads in Anshan City. Solve the problem of traffic jam
of AISC's production & staff transportation, reduce traffic load near area of railway station,
thoroughly eliminate the confusion and crowded situation of Anshan urban traffic.
Shorten the time and distance of traveling of pedestrians and MV & NMV vehicles, favorable
to improve the life quality of public.
Arrange the resettled residents in the neighborhood and incorporate tihe dismantled enterprises
into the appropriate industrial zones, to improve living environment of displaced residents,
make the city arrangement more reasonable and raise the living quality of public of the whole
city.
In large range, the negative impact of traffic noise wvith JRR is less than that of without JRR;
the impact of vehicle emission on air environment is larger than the existing situation. but the
increasing rate is less than that of without JRR. Compared with the existing situation, the
increasing rate of air pollutants of with or without JRR is shown in Table 7-1.
When the project is completed. the density of pollutants in the air at most road sections is
low-er than that of without JRR.
Moving of tram line will solve the problem of mutual interference of vehicles and tramcars.
The interference occurs mainin in front of Anshan Railway Station. at Jianguo Road section
*                    from Rainbow Bridge to Wuyi Road Intersection and at area near Lishan Underpass. In the
meantime. the negative impact of tramcar noise on the residents along the line will be
reduced.
.3



Liaoning Urban Transport Project-Anshan Subproject      Environmental Impact Assessment
3.3 Negative Impact
In construction phase, normal traveling of vehicle and pedestrians will be negatively impacted,
and the living of the residents near the construction site will also be affected.
The project will occupy 44350 m2 cultivated land which can never be restored, and 103231
m2 green area (among which 57.38% of trees to be cut down are over 25 years old) will be
destroyed.
When the project is completed. it is not convenient for the public to cross the street. Due to
increased vehicle flow and speed, the impact of traffic noise on buildings adjacent to the road
sides will be more seriqus than the existing situation.
The density of air pollutants in the area of Laodong Road will be higher than that of without
JRR in 2010.
The negative impact in the view of vibration, surface water and sunshine will not be greater
than that of without JRR, and the impact of solid waste disposal during construction phase on
environment is very little.
4 MITIGATION MEASURES FOR SERIOUS IMPACTS
4.1 Design Phase
*  Traffic light for pedestrians crossing street shall be added at the intersections where the
public crosses the street frequently. Traffic policeman box shall be added on Jianguo
Road section in front of gate of Sifangtai Fruit Wholesale Market where there is heavy
flow of customers and vehicles to facilitate the pedestrians crossing street and vehicles
turning left.
*  By many times of discussions and agreement with ARPO, Anshan Urban and
tountryside Planning Institute and Beijing Municipal Project Design & Research
Institute, two sound barriers 3 m high and 250 m long shall be installed respectively on
the both sides of approach of Wuyi Road Interchange's section near Wuyi Road Primary
School.
*  91 air-conditioners shall be installed in the patient ward and diagnosis room of three
hospitals such as Hospital of Grain Bureau etc.; 262 air conditioners shall be installed in
the classrooms of 5 schools Neighboring the project road; 5094 air-conditioners shall be
installed in the residential buildings Neighboring the project road in order to reduce noise
pollution in summer.
*  By agreement with the design institution, the original space of Sm between the trees on
both sides of the street shall be changed to 2.5m, in order to restore the green area
destroyed by the project as soon as possible. In 2010 all the destroyed green area can be
restored.
4



Liaoning Urban Transport Project-Anshan Subproject     Environmental Impact Assessment
4.2 Construction Phase
APRO must clarify the environmental protection responsibility during the construction and
transportation while entrusting the contractor with the project and must incorporate the
responsibility in the contract.
The construction shall be accomplished section by section and half by half at main places
such as AISC entrance; temporary passageways shall be set up during construction phase.
Designated person shall fetch pupils to cross the street when construction is being made near
schools.
The construction timne shall be shortened; construction at night shall be avoided; construction
equipment and facilit-&es of lower noise shall be used; operation at night of machinery with
high noise and vibration must be approved by Anshan Environment Protection Btireau.
By bulk transportation, the material must be covered and the transportation should avoid peak
hours of traffic; water sprinkling times should be added on the way; the site of construction
should have temporary store houses for bulk material; when old buildings or structures are
dismantled, plastic fence should be set up around building in order to suppress dust emission
to the environment.
In construction phase, Anshan Environmental Monitoring Center shall carry out monitoring
of noise, air, surface water and so on during construction phase.
4.3 Operational Phase
Anshan City has solemnly promised to develop and implement motor vehicle emission
control strategy (MVECS) to avoid deterioration of environment resulting from increase of
vehicles after 2010. For details. see Annex 3.
Vehicles must be inspected annually and randomly: the vehicles of high noise and emission
which are beyond standard must be brought under control within the specified time. The
vehicles of high noise and emission which are beyond standard must not run.
Anshan Environmental Monitoring Center will carry out monitoring of noise, air, vibration
and surface water related to the project.
5 PLAN OF ENVIRONMENTAL MONITORING AND
MANAGEMENT
The'administrative institutions shall be staffed by one or two full-time environmental
protection personnel to ensure the responsibility of daily management. accepting complaints
concerning environmental impact. handling pollution cases as well as controlling and
coordinating the monitoring activities on motor vehicles emission and traffic noise which are
conducted by Anshan Environment Monitoring Center and Anshan Vehicle Inspecting
Station.
The project shall be managed successively by ARPO during the phase of construction and bN



Liaoning Urban Transport Project-Anshan Subproject     Environmental Impact Assessment
the AUCB in the operational phase. The environmental monitoring ( including the air, noise.
vibration and surface water etc.) shall be managed by the Anshan Environmental Monitoring
Center.
A monitoring plan, five years for the construction period and three years for the operational
phase, is envisaged for the project, refer to Table 5-3, 5-4 and Fig.5-1, 5-2 about the
monitoring items and monitoring points, the environmental monitoring cost totals 0.7534
million Yuan RMB . For the successful implementation of environmental protection
measures, a training program is proposed to train Project Office staff and contractors, and two
officials from the Project Office shall be trained abroad for 30 days by a qualified overseas
training institution, the 20 project contractors shall be trained by the AEPB for 10 days. the
training cost totals 0.2063 millionYuan RMB and the training content is shown in Table 5-1.
6 SUMMARY OF ASSESSMENT CONCLUSION
Two public investigations have been carried out in EIA. The second social investigation to
the public demonstrates that 97.8% of 456 persons including peddlers to be moved from
Yongchang Market to Sandao Street Market think the impact of the project on them shall be
reduced to the acceptable degree if the mitigation measures are executed. The other 2.2%
express indifferent attitude to the mitigation measures.
Anshan Environment Monitoring Center who will carry out environmental monitoring and
vehicle inspecting of this project is one of the best environmental organization with rich
experience and modern equipment in Liaoning Provincz and is able to complete the above
mentioned work. By consultation with Anshan municipal government, the environmental
administrative organization recommended in EIA report during construction and operational
phase is feasible.
Based on achievement in different topics, the EIA report recognizes that the positive impact
on environment of JRR project is greater than the negative one. The project has reasonable
effect to improve environmental quality of Anshan City. The selected alignment of the project
is reasonable, the project is feasible from the view of environmental protection.

1 INTRODUCTION
1.1 Objective and Indicators
1.1.1 Objective
The project is a component of Liaoning urban traffic comprehensive rectification program.
For Anshan project geographic location, see Fig.1-1. According to China's Environmental
Protection Regulation for Constructional Engineering. Anshan Renewal Project Office
(ARPO) has entrusted us to provide this report.
Based on results of,social investigation and present environment quality monitoring, on
characteristics of urban  traffic  reconstruction  engineering, the  report provides a
comprehensive and systematic analysis of positive and negative influences to Anshan's
natural and social environment when the project was constructed and put into operation
according to the preferred alignment or alternatives. It also makes measures to mitigate and
compensate negative influences of the project. points out the feasibility of the project
considering environment protection and gives proposal to make a plan of environmental
administration and monitoring.
1.1.2 Indicators
Objective: Improve maintenance and environmental sustainability.
Goal: Environmental protection of the project area
Strategy 1: Establish and implement an EAP and monitoring program
Indicator: Annual monitoring results for air quality and noise as per the EAP
Strategy 2: Develop and implement a long-term motor vehicle emission control
strategy(MVECS) to mitigate citywide imlpacts on air quality.
Indicator: Development ot'a MVCES for Anshan City by July 2001.
(date to be confirmed during Appraisal).
Indicator: Adoption and imnplementation of the MVEC'S(including an InspecEion
and Maintenance Program) for Anshan City. with specific targets, by July
2002.(Date to be confirmed during Appraisal).
Indicator: Annual reporting on performance of MVECS.

2 PROJECT DESCRIPTION AND ENGINEERING ANALYSIS
2.1 General
The subproject consists of five components of road infrastructure, traffic management. public
transport, road maintenance and technical assistance & training. The project description is
divided into two components according to the extent of the potential environmental impact.
A) Components with potential environmental impact
1) Extension of South Ring Road
South Ring Road shall extended 1.34 km eastward from Glass Factory, including construction
of Dongshao Underpass, belt railway Underpass and a viaduct. This road shall be four-slab
road and 50 m width of redline; Zhonghua Road shall be widened and extended 0.46 km to
south, starting from Changdian Street and ending at South Ring Road. This road shall be one-
slab and 40 m width of redline: Yuanlin Road shall be reconstructed and extended 1.40 km.
This road shall be three-slab and 50 m width of redline.
2) Huangang Road and Yongchang Street
A three-layer full-directional interchange (no limit of traffic direction) shall be built at
intersection of Wuyi Road and Jianguo Road, Huangang Road and Yongchang Street shall be
widened, totaling 4.26 km in length, three-slab and 42 m width of redline. Wuyi Road
Interchange shall cross over Zhongchang Railway in east-west and connect with Jianguo
Road in south-north.
3) South Jianguo Road and North Jianguo Road
Jianguo Road shall be constructed and widened from South Ring Road (Sifangtai Interchange)
to East Jianguo Road, including construction of underpass under belt railway, Minsheng Road
viaduct, Lishan Street viaduct. This road shall be three-slab and 50 m width of redline,
totaling 8.6 km in length; Laodong Road shall be widened from Jianguo Road to Hebei Road,
including construction of bridge over Shahe River. This road shall be three-slab and 40 m
width of redline, totaling 1.77 km in length.
4) Hebei Road
The proposed Hebei Road starts from Jianguo Road and ends at Shengli Road, which passes
through residential area of Shahe village. This road shall be three-slab and 42 m width of
redline, totaling 1.05 km.
5) Tram line movement
The tram line to be changed starts from Anshan Railway Station and ends at Laodong Road.
the length totaling. 5.2 km. The existing tram line will be moved westoAard and the moved
12



Liaoning Urban Transport Project-Anshan Subproject       Environmental Impact Assessment
tram line will go through the Eryijiu Rd., Zhanqian Square, Yijingxiang Underpass, Lishan
Underpass, Anquan St., Lishan Railway Station, Lishan Turnaround. Viaducts at Sankong
Bridge and Lishan Underpass shall be built along the tramline.
6) Off-street parking
The station in front of railway station to be built shall occupy the area of about 5000 m2 and
2
hold max. 96 vehicles; People's Park station, 8000 m , max. 157 vehicles; Hunan station,
1320 m2, 37 vehicles. This project involves road, water drainage, greening and lighting.
7) Bus transfer station
To convenient AISC's employees and reduce the ratio of AISC's employees who cycle to
work, a bus transfer station, occupying the area of 7706 m2, shall be set up under Wuyi Road
Interchange.
8) Reconstruction of Hongqi Road
Hongqi Road maintenance project consists of Hongqi Road (Lingshan Road - junction of
Zhongchang railway) and Laodong Road (junction of Zhongchang railway - Shahe Bridge),
4003 m in length.
b) Components with minor or non environmental impact
I) Bus only road
Shengli Road and Renmnin Road is the main trunk where there are many bus lanes and large
p-onle flow. 6 bus lanes is on Shengli Road and 12 on Renaming Road now. To improve
public transport and reflect the principle of preference for public transport, Shengli Road bus
special lane (Shifu Square - Lishan Square). Renaming bus only road (Jiudao Street in Tiexi
district - Jianguo Road) and Zhonghua Road tram/bus only road shall be set up.
2) Channalization of intersections
The following intersections are selected to be channalized according to the conditions of
traffic jam at intersections and bus traffic volume:
WuIvi Rd./ Dongshan St.
Jianshen Rd./ Yuanlin Rd.
Sandao St. in Tiexi district/ Minsheng Rd.

Y'uanlin Rd.! Luhua St.
Yuanlin Rd./ Gongnong St.
Eryijiu Rd./ Zhonghua Rd.
3) Traffic signal improvement
There are existing 49 traffic light controlled intersections in the city. It is envisaged in the
project that 41 more intersections shall be provided with traffic lights and the traffic lights for
pedestrians and cyclist shall also be provided. The traffic lights for cyclist totaling 23 will be
mainly distributed on the three-slab roads, while the traffic lights for pedestrians totaling 20
will be mainly distributed on the down Anshan and the exits of AISC.
Due to the fact that most of the traffic light facilities become obsolete, it is envisaged that 36
traffic light facilities shall be improved. After the improvement, the number of traffic light
controlled intersections will reach 90, which accounts for 50% of the number of the main
intersections of Anshan.
4) Traffic sign and marking
1364 traffic signs and markings shall be improved or newly erected, including 480 instruction
signs, 359 prohibition signs, 223 warning signs, 267 guideposts and 35 bridge nameplates.
5) Pedestrian physical separator
Pedestrian physical separator totaling 18.4 km in length shall be provided in the bustling
business area such as downtown area, Renmin Rd. business area, Renmin Department Store,
Diandi Department Store, and Lishan Department Store.
6)-Median separator
Median separator totaling 16.6km in length shall be provided on Jianguo Rd., Huangang Rd.,
Yongchang St. and south section of the Yuanlin Rd..
7) NMV exclusive road
It is envisaged in the project that Zhengyi St., Youai St., Lishan St. and Guangming St. shall
be used exclusively by NMV.
8) Pedestrian sidewalk
Sidewalk totaling 62946 m2 in area shall be provided on Jiaotong Rd., Shuguang Rd.,
Shengou Rd., Sandao- St. in Tiexi district, hunan district and Erdao St. with respect to the
roa.d conditions.

9) TA and training
It shall include the MVECS, other TA and training items.
2.1.1 Present Status of Anshan's Road Traffic
Anshan is a heavy industrial city. The plant area of Anshan Iron & Steel Complex (AISC,
employees 0.2 million) is concentrated on the northwest to the city, occupying 1/4 land of the
city. Eighty-seven percent of city's total employees are working in industrial enterprises.
Table 2-1 and Fig.2-1 show the present status of Anshan's road traffic.

2.1.2 Role of the Project in Traffic General Planning
According to traffic flows and tendency of population growth, Anshan municipal government
has made an Anshan Urban Traffic Development Program valid until 2025. The program has
established a skeleton of urban traffic network shown in Fig.2-2. It is a rapid speed road
system  like the Chinese letter   '41". Based on this skeleton, supported by some corridors and
combining a number of branch ways, Anshan's chessboardwise and radiated road network
will be formed in the future.
As a part of outer frame ;".fi' (outer circle road ), the South Ring Road, West Ring Road and
North Ring Road were principally implemented. The roads at four ends of "+" from  "`P"
(east, south, west and north of the city ) were also finished (see Fig.2-2). The project mainly
concerns the -1" skeleton whichi is the key part tor realization of Anshan Urban Traffic
Development Program.

2.1.3 Preferred Alignment and Alternatives
2.1.3.1 Preferred Alignment
The project which shall involve a road section of 18.87 knm in total length, includes Jianguo
Road's (south-north) widening and extension to north: construction of Hebei Road to connect
the northern exit of the city; widening and reconstruction of Huangang Road (east-west) and
Yongchang Street (east-west); construction of Wuyi Road Interchange as main crossing at the
meeting point of Huangang Road with Yongchang Street; widening. reconstruction and
extension to south of Yuanlin Road and Zhonghua Road to connect South Ring Road which
will be extended to east; movement (required by widening of Jianguo Road) of tram line (now
located at Jianguo Road and its west side) to the west close to Zhongchang Railway.

2.1.3.2 Alternatives
a) Jianguo Road Alternative (A)
Since the preferred alignment brings more work of demolition and resettlement, occupation of
green vegetation at east side of northern Jianguo Road and difficulty in construction
management, the designer proposed a scheme of widening Jianguo Road's southern part
(South Ring Road- Wuyi Road ) and making its northern part (Wuyi Road - entrance of
Laodong Road ) to an elevated road.
The related road with a total length of 4.2 km and a width of 17 m will be constructed over
the original tram line. Two direction-limited interchanges will be built up at Lishan
Underpass and Guangming Street (east gate .of AISC ) to solve the problem of motor vehicle
traffic of AISC. Another interchange of same type will be erected at Heping Road to connect
the related road with roads to city center.
The main function of the related road is to facilitate motor vehicles traffic between all
districts of the city. The present northern Jianguo Road keeps unchanged, serving as a special
route for public omnibuses.
b) Hebei Road Alternative (B)
According to the preferred alignment, the Hebei Road connecting Laodong Road with
Shengli Road is a new construction going through the present single-story-house residential
zone. The alternative suggests that the existing Shahe Street on the north of the zone replaces
the Hebei Road. The beginning of Shahe Street is the north of and 250 m apart from proposed
Hebei Road. The Shahe Street goes 814 m in the direction of northeast. turns with a length of
615 m to southeast and then meets Shengli Road. It connects also Jiancai Street which is
planned to be built on the east of Shengli Road. The altemnative requires reasonable
reconstruction of Shahe Street. distance from red lines shall be 30 m and width of road
without separation strip shall be 15 m (See Fig.2-3).
c)' .outh Ring Road Alternaftie (C')
According to the preferred alignment, a section of South Ring Road (the Glass Factorv --
Yuanlin Road) will pass through the Zhendong Metal Structure Factory. According to the
alternative, this section will be a detour on the south of the plant where Yuanlin Road makes
a curve (See Fig.2-3).
d) Shahe River Bridlge Alle nacuive (D)
The-preferred alignment determines demolition of Shahe River Bridge (Laodong Road
Bridge ) and build-up of a newx one at the same place.
The alternative suggests that the old bridge keeps unclhanoed and the new one will be buiit up
on the west of the old one. x%ith a distance of 25.56 m. 'I'he length and width of the nevw-
bridge are according to the stipulatiotn of the preferred alignmlient.
The alternative will result in turn1illne of Laodonc Road on hoth sides of Shahe River to meet
23



Liaoning Urban Transport Project-Anshan Subproject                         Environmental Impact Assessment
the new bridge and bring extra requirement of demolition and resettlement in the zone nearby
the ends of bridge (see Fig.2-3).
e) Summary of alternatives
Except differences from preferred alignment mentioned above. other contents (including the
movement of tram line) of the alternatives are the same like contents of the preferred
alignment.

will help in improving traffic conditions of Anshan city to a great extent. For brief

2.2 Schedule
Design schedule
The fea: ibility study has been finished by the end of May. 1998.
24



Liaoning Urban Transport Project-Anshan Subproject                  Environmental Impact Assessment
The preliminary design shall be finished at the end of Nov. 1998 and detailed design shall be
finished at the end of Feb. 1999.
Construction schedule
a) The extension of the southern part shall be completed first. that includes: reconstruction of
Yuanlin Road (1-3-1), extension and new construction of road ( 1-3-2), widening of
Zhonghua Road ( 1-2-1). reconstruction of road ( 1-2-2) and construction of sections of
South Ring Road from Glass Factory to Zhonghua Road (1-1-1) and from Zhonghua Road
to Yuanlin Road (1-1-2).
b)After finish of engineering concerning southern roads, the traffic on Jianguo Road will be
transferred to the Yianlin Road and South Ring Road, so the comprehensive reconstruction
of Jianguo Road could start. Simultaneously, the Yongchang Street and Huangang Road
can be widened.
c)After completion of construction of Jianguo Road, Yongchang Street and Huangang Road,
start the reconstruction of Laodong Road Bridge, finally start the construction of Hebei
Road.
According to the feasibility study. the project will last 5 years, the construction will begin in
Feb. 1999.

2.4 Motor Vehicle Fleet
2.4.1 Current Population and Expected Growth
Anshan City with a total area of 9251 km2 has now a population of 3.3125 million, exercises
jurisdiction over Haicheng City, Taian County and Xiuyan County. The urban area is of
624.29 km2 (completed zone 1 14 kn2 ).
Land use in different phases and expected population growth of Anshan City in planning zone,
construction zone (including Tiedong District, Tiexi District, Lishan District, Jiupu
subdistrict and Shahe subdistrict ) are shown in Table 2-8.
2.4.2 Traffic Forecast
With an average growth rate of 13.5% from 1991 to 1995 and a growth rate of 6.05% from
1995 to 1996, the actual amount of motor vehicles in Anshan City has reached 64798 at the
end of 1996. According to the forecast made by Anshan Vehicle Administration Office, the
annual growth rate of vehicles will be of 6% in the future. Table 2-9 and Table 2-10 show
the kinds and growth expectation of motor vehicles. The constitution of road network in the

3 PRESENT ENVIRONMENTAL CONDITIONS
3.1 Physical Setting
-AII the engineering of the project wvill occur in the urban area of the city.
Anshan City is located at 122 '  123 ° E and 40 - - 4i 4    N. in the middle of Liaoning
Province. It is 89 km in the south of Shengyang. 308 knm in the north of Dalian, 120 km of
Yingkou Bayuquan port. The Zhongchang Railway passes the city from south to north and the
Shenyang-Dalian Expressway passes the city in the western. There is an air port on the
southwest of the ciV where the flight to Beijing. Guangzhou, Fushan, Huizhou etc. is
available. Fig. I - I shows the geographical position of Anshan.
The Qianshan Mountain is located on the east of the city. On the west, Anshan is conjunct
with the alluvial plain via rivers of Liaohe, Hunhe and Taizihe. The southeast part of the city
is higher while the northwest part is lower. Elevation of construction sections of the project is
between 25.8 m and 57.6 m.
From N-E to S-W, the thickness of underground base rock covered mainly by the sediment of
Quaternary System varies graduallv greater (from 20 ni to 55 m). The baserock in the north of
Anshan railway station consists principally of Liaohe group of strata while in the south of
Anshan railway station mainly of limestone of Cambrian System. The following shows the
sequence of baserock distribution from N-E to S-W.
* Granite of Archaean Era
*  Metamorphous feldspar-silicarenite, dimicaceous-schist and sericite-schist of Liaohe
group of strata
* Sinian System silicarenite and Cambrian System limestone with intercalation of dolomite
limestone, marlite and shale
The underground water is of the following kinds:
* Perched water over the sediment of Quatemary System
* Baserock crevice water
* Karst fracture water
The underground water is principally of calcium bicarbonate type with a mineralization
degree of less than lg/L, supplemented by precipitation and subsurface flows, applied in the
way of pumping.
3.2 Biophysical Environment
3.2.1 Meteorology and Climate
Anshan City is located in the warm temperate region of continental monsoon climate. In
summer, south wind is dominant. temperature is rather high, air is humid and rain occurs
often. In winter that lasts as long as 6 months, north wind is dominant, temperature is low and
there is few precipitation. In spring. it is dry and windy, sunshine time is long, evaporativity is
28



Liaoning Urban Transport Project-Anshan Subproject                   Environmental Impact Assessment
high and humidity is low. The autumn is short and pleasantly cool, wind and rain occur now
and then.
Meteorological parameters collected in recent years are shown in Table 3-1.
Table 3-1 Meteorological Parameters of Anshan
Item       Temperature  |  Precipitation   1Relative humidity |  Sunshine time   |  Wind speed
Annual average    10.7 C         929.4 mm           63 %           2617.2 hrs         2.6 mls
Average temperature in the hottest month ( Jul.): 23.6 'C.
Average temperature in the coldest month (Jan.): -5.4 'C.

Table 3-4 demonstrates that there is no excess vibration except VLZIo value that exceeds 2
dB when monitoring at 7:30 and 12:00. This means the motor vehicles produce less vibration
influence to sensitive points at both roadsides.
3.2.3 Air Quality
Anshan is a heavy industrial city and its air pollution is more severe. Among the industrial
enterprises, Anshan Iron and Steel Co. is the largest air pollution source. The emission of
smoke and dust, S02, NOx, and CO have separately made up 63%, 81%, 92% and 87% of the
whole city. The emission of exhaust gas from main air pollution sources of the whole city is
168432.6 Mm3/a while the emission of the above pollutants are 185100 t/a, 78100 t/a, 57800
t/a and 7000 t/a separately.

3.2.3.2 Monitoring of Present Status
For this environmental assessment, the air environmental quality monitoring was carried out
at 8 monitoring points in the non-heating period (Oct.26 to Nov.1,1996) and the heating
period (Dec.20 to 26,1996) by Anshan Environmental Monitoring Center on the basis of
related national regulations. obtaining 8092 effective monitoring data. For the distribution of
monitoring places see Fig.2-1. For the monitoring statistical results see Table 3-6 to Table 3-
9, Fig.3-5 and Fig.3-6. All the above tables perform "Air Environmental Quality Standard"
GB3095-1996, formally executed on Oct.1, 1996.
It can be seen from the monitoring results that Anshan air environmental quality is poor. the
hourly concentration of all pollution factors has exceeded the standard, the daily average
values have exceeded the standard, in which the excess rates of HC and B[a]P are 100%.
3.2.4 Surface Water Quality
This project is only involved w ith South Shahe River in the north of Anshan urban area. This
river is a seasonal one, taking its source at Qianshan Mountain in the southeast of Anshan. It
mainly receives domestic sewage in the north of Anshan urban area and the treated industrial
waste water of AISC Qidashan Concentrator and AISC north plant area. At present, the water
is mainly used for the agricultural irrigation.

precipitation and dust falling. But in general, the investigated soil is not polluted by the land
users except that (polluted by oil) used by the Machinery Repair Plant of AISC Construction
Co. and two small-sized private motorcycle repair shops.
In addition of infrastructure. three public parking stations (Hunan station, People's Park
station, station in front of railway station) and a new bus depot (No.16 line bus) shall be set
p. The_places occupied belong to land reserved for urban construction application, mainly
with ground surface of cement or asphalt and occasionally with some buildings. According to
site survey and investigation, the soil is not polluted by land users and the land is used for
public applications. The heavy repair of Hongqi Road will be carried out on the basis of
road's original foundation and shall not bring change of original land application.
3.2.5.2 Assessment of Vegetation Present Status
On-site prospecting and investigation of vegetation along both project's roadsides have been
conducted. The results in details are shown in Table 3-13.
Table 3-13 shows a good present status of vegetation along both project's roadsides that
flowers, grass, trees or shrubbery are planted at places where the planting is feasible. Among
th& trees, poplar and willow are dominant. Over 60% of the trees are 25 years old or older,
which lost branches during heavy rainfalls and winds. Typically trees over 25 years will be
cut and replaced with young trees in Anshan City.
In the construction of parking stations and bus depot, no green land and trees are related. In
the engineering of Hongqi Road reconstruction (road widening), near 100 trees (more than 20
years old) shall be cut down which takes 50% of trees already available.

population is sparse. All the people living along the road are non-agricultural population.

place of pedestrians and vehicles.

4 ENVIRONMENTAL IMPACT ANALYSIS
4.1 Introduction
The following items were analyzed in this paper in accordance with the "Oudline
Environmental Inpact .na/vsJi- approved by the National 1-nvironmental Protection Agency.
"TOR approved by the World Bank and the concern of the public.
* Noise and Vibration
* Air Quality
* Water Quality
* Landscape and Ecology
*  Socio-economic.Components
* Sunshine
* Alternatives
The patterns below shall be followved to the best of Author's ability (in construction and
operation).
* Approach and Methodology
*  Vehicle Emissions Inventory
* Impact Analysis
*  Mitigation
* Residual Impact
The impact of preferred alignment and alternatives oni environmental, with or without project.
were described and compared.
4.2 Impact Analysis of Noise and Vibration
4.2.1 Approach
4.2.1.1 Noise
The speed of motor vehicles X0ill. upon the completion of the project, reach 38.49 km/h. as
compared to existing 33.76 kmn:h. 'I'he project will ease the traffic jam significantly. however.

4.2.1.2 Vibration *
As mentioned hereinbefore, there are two schemes for the project, i.e., widening and
elevating schemes. The latter wvill produce more vibration, therefore more impact than the
former. The proposed elevated road lies on the west side of Jianguo Road, 50 m away from
the nearest sensitive points. So. the elevated road will produce very little impact on sensitive
area. The monitoring on current st.Atus shows that the vibration level of Jianguo Road at
different time period didn't exceed the limit.
As required by "Outline Environment Impact Analysis" and its review provided by State
Bureau of Environmental Protection, the impact analysis on vibration in current and
operational phases shall be made, the prediction calculation on traffic vibration is left out of
consideration.

team choice as well as equipment which shall be used in the construction. Some equipment
are only for reference because they shall not definitely be used in the future. As indicated in
Table 4-7, the noise levels at 50 m from the construction equipment exceed the night
standard (55 dB). Because the roads to be constructed are adjacent to the residential buildings,
these equipment is forbidden at night.

According to Table 4-2 and GB12523-90, the noise levels at different distance (5-50 m)

mixer, wheel crane, pneumatic hammer and rock drill.

Table 4-9 shows that noise level on both road sides after completion of JRR will mostly
exceed the standard, see Table 4-10 and Fig.4-2.
According to "Environmental ANoise Standard ofAnshan Cit 'v . all the noise levels beside the
red lines of all sections except some in peak hours and daNtime. exceed the standard. The
peak hour noise level exceeds the standard IV by 0.7 - 9.6 dB, the daytime noise level
exceed the standard A,' by 0.2 - 8.8 dB. the nighttime noise level exceeds the standard IV
by 3.3 - 13.1 dB. Almost all the noise level of difference zones within 20 - 100 m of the
road exceed the standard to large extent. The section that suffers the most serious noise is
Section 3-5, whose noise level exceeds the standard by 14.8 dB in peak hours, 14.0 dB in
daytime and 14.4 dB in- nighttime.
(2) Noise prediction analysis in the year of 2010 without project
The model employed prediction points selected and prediction period selected in the year of
2010, without project are exactly the same as that of the year of 2010, with project. For the
prediction results see Table 4-11 and Fig.4-3.
As Table 4-11 shows, with the project, the noise levels of the area near the red line, except
that of section 2-3 South Shengli Road and North Shengli Road, exceed the standard. Without
the project, the noise levels in difference zones within 20-lOOm of the road is similar to that
of with project.
(5) Noise level in the year of 2010. with vs. without project
Comparison was made based on the prediction results. The values in the Table 4-12 and
Fig.4-4 were the difference of with vs without project.
The purpose of predicting the noise levels of South Shengli Road, North Shengli Road and
Renmnin Road that are out of the scope of the project is to demonstrate the impact of the
project on the road of the city. We can conclude that in the year of 2010.
The noise levels of South Shengli Road and Renmin Road during the day and at night, with
project, are decreased by 2.1 and 1.6 dB, the max. respectively, as compared to that of
without project, which shows that the project has good impact on the urban area. South
Shengli Road and Renmin Road are chosen to represent other non-project roads. After
completion of JRR project, vehicles on other roads such as South Shengli Road and Renmin
Road shall be attracted to travel on the project road. Traffic flow and noise level from vehicle
on other roads shall be reduced. Therefore, the overall noise level in the city on traffic trunks
shall be accordingly decreased.
The noise level of section 1-2, with project is lower than that without project. There are three
reasons of serious status of noise level on road section 1-2 (extension of Zhonghua Road)
vehicles on Yuanlin Road have to pass this section to enter South Ring Road, vehicles
traveling on this section are most of heavy-duty ones (there are many plants in this zone);
high frequency of stop-start of vehicle due to bad road paving.
The noise level of section 3-4 at nighttime, with project, is lower than that without project.

( Analysis of noise impact brought out by the tramcar line changing
The tramcar line to be changed starts from Anshan Railway Station and ends at the meeting
point of Laodong- Road with Ligong Street, the length totaling 5200 m. The noise levels
before and after changing the line remain the same. Residential area is on the east side of the
project road. As the tramcar line is moved 5-60 m westwards. the tramcar line is far away
from sensitive points on the east side of Jianguo Road..
The section of tramcar line (Lishan Underpass-Ligong Street) will be moved from Laodong
Road to Anquan Street. The existing track is 6 m away from the first row of buildings on
roadsides, the distance will be increased to 12-15 m after the moving. On the both sides of
Laodong RoaU, there are residential areas. On the east side of Anquan Street, there are
residential areas while on its west side there are Changda railway and AISC plant area.
Therefore, the residents affected by traffic noise shall be reduced if the tramcar line is moved
to Anquan Street. The noise pollution is accordingly transferred to area neighboring Anquan
Street. The noise impact imposed on the first row of building at Laodong Road and Anquan
Street by tramcar are shown in Table 4-15.
Table 4-15 Noise Impact of Tramcar along Laodong Road and Anquan Street

than the current residents dwelling along Laodong Road after the tramline is moved.
Although the noise pollution at Anquan Street will be more serious, the line changing project,
from the point of view of whole city's road network. will reduce the range and extent of noise
impact on the city.

b) Vibration impact analysis
With respect to the monitoring results of current vibration. the vibration levels of motor
vehicles running on Jianguo Rd. do not exceed the standard at any time, which means a slight
impact on along the line.
The project, which comprises dominantly of widening and newr building of ground roads. will
produce less impact on surrounding environment. With respect to the "Outline Environmental
Impact Assessment" and its review. no prediction and analysis on vibration impact shall be
made.
The vibration proquced by running motor vehicles. in brief, will not exert big impact on
surrounding environment after the project is completed and put into operation.
4.2.4 Mitigation
4.2.4.1 Construction Phase
a) Noise mitigation in construction
During road construction most of the noise generated shall exceed the specific figures in the
Noise Standard on construction site. Because the noise is inevitable during the construction,
in order to reduce the noise impact on the surrounding environment, the following measures
shall be taken to mitigate the impact.
(I) No operation of equipment such as, impact piling machine, pneumatic hammer, drill etc.
which generate high noise is allowed at night (22:00--6:00 next day).
(2) Low noise equipment or equipment with acoustic device shall be used and the impact
piling machine, generator etc. shall be equipped with muffler.
(3) The construction department should make good arrangement for construction time and
site. The high noise equipment should be placed far from the sensitive area and maintained
periodically to ensure the operation of the equipment.
(4) A temporary sound isolating fence structure or sound absorbing and isolating barrier must
be installed at the site which is seriously affected by the noise produced by the construction
machinery to minimize the noise pollution to the surrounding areas. The fence structure must
be adopted to isolate noise when construction is carried out near Wuyi Road Primary School,
Old People Palace, etc. which are the sound environment protection objects.
(5) Some building structures should be precast in the proper place outside of the urban area as
much as possible, then be brought to the site for installation. During construction of Wuyi
Road and Minsheng Road Interchanges, the large precast structures should be mainly installed
at site.
b) Vibration mitigation in construction phase
To mitigate the vibration affecting the surrounding environment in construction phase, the

(2) Reasonable plan anld arrangen2ent for the lcantl of loth .sides of road
© The planned distance from the new buildings on both sides of the main line to the red line
of road should be no less than 20 m. It is recommended to set up afforestation isolating zone

(Z For the reconstructed area where the newly built Hebei Road, Zhonghua Road and

comply with the regional environmental quality standard according to the requirements of
division of area with different noise ievels.
(I The first row buildings along the two sides of the trunk line are not suitable to be used for
noise sensitive places such as schools, hospitals, kindergarten etc.. These organizations are
not suitable to be built in 100 mn from the red line of the road. The first row buildings along
the road are suitable to be used as commercial shop. car parking, etc. which are not sensitive
to noise. In this way, not only the land can be fully used, but also the noise impact on the
sensitive objects can be reduced.
(i) The first row buildings along the road should be parallel to the road. This may mitigate the
impact of traffic noise on the buildings behind them.
(3) Installation of noise barrier along the rcad
The noise barrier shall be determined by the professional design institution. When making
decision of barrier's location. type, and material etc., many factors such as neighboring
buildings shape and noise level. road structure, weathering resistance and safety of barrier and
landscape of the city shall be taken into consideration.
According to the experiences at home and abroad. the noise barrier shall be installed on the
two sides of elevated road. Based on engineering characteristic of JRR project, the following
points are recommended.
®  No noise barrier installation along the ground road
The distance between sensitive objects greatly affected by the traffic noise and the first motor
vehicle lane shall be over 15 m. Since the two sides of the road have very close connection,
the residents along the road are not willing to obstruct the connection between two sides in
accordance with the public opinions. The individual protection against noise of sensitive
objects shall be adopted to minimize the traffic noise pollution instead of installation of noise

Analysis of options
Sound barrier
To attain better noise reducing effect, sound barrier (advertisement board) must have
adequate length and height and opening must not be in it, or noise isolating effect will be
lowered. On one hand, implementation of this option shall affect going & coming of residents
and lighting, cut connections between both sides of the road; on the other hand, investment of
this option is very high, 7200 Yuan RMB per running meter of 3-meter-high sound barrier.
Sound-absorbing road
Anshan City is a heavily industrial city with much dust and snowfall in winter, which shall
result in clogging of sound-absorbing holes and then spoil sound-absorbing effect of sound-
absorbing road. Cost of sound-absorption road is very high and no sound-absorption roads
have been used successfully in the northeast of China.
Separation belt for greening
The distance between residential buildings and red line of the project road is 0-20 m. It is
introduced that noise is reduced by only 3 dB for separation belt 50 m wide. Because no
buffer zone over 50 m wide is on the both side of the project road, it is impossible to
implement this option.

is required to take vibration protective measures into full consideration when designing the

4.2.5 Impact After Implementation of Mitigation Measures
4.2.5.1 Construction Phase
During the construction of the project. the operationi of mechanical equipment shall cause
noise and vibration thus affecting the surrounding environment. Since the road construction is
just a short term action, the impact of noise and vibration on the surrounding sensitive points
is temporary. As longk as the construction team observes the construction rules and takes the
mitigation measures, the impact generated by the construction equipment on the sensitive
points in the surrounding area shall be effectively mitigated.
The construction team must take practical measures to mitigate noise and vibration based on
the features of construction and the distribution of sensitive points under the strict supervision
of environmental protection and city construction departments.
4.2.5.2 Operational phase
a) Noise
(1) Analysis of sensitive point affected by noise
Noise at most sensitive points in various noise areas along the project road shall exceed the
standard. In Anshan, the buildings are provided with double glazing windows which isolate
noise efficiently, thus being favorable to mitigate the noise impact on the sensitive points.
The sensitive points such as Tianhe Mansion, Global Hotel, etc. shall be affected greatly by
the traffic noise. However, these buildings are provided with better noise isolating facilities
(glass enclosure. double glazing windows, air conditioners. etc. ) so that there is less impact
on the inner living environment.
The residential building, schools and hospitals neighboring the project road are important
sensitive points in this project. The effective measures to reduce noise impact shall be taken,
that is, air-conditioner shall be installed in the schools and hospitals and air-conditioner shall
be installed in the residential buildings neighboring the project road.
(2) Noise conditions of different sensitive points after realization of mitigation measures
All the sensitive buildings in Anshan are provided with double glazing windows. Using
double glazing windows is favorable to reduce noise impact.
The following mitigation measures shall be taken for the noise sensitive points neighboring
the project road: air-conditioners shall be installed in the schools and hospitals neighboring
the project road exceeding the noise standard; air-conditioners shall be installed in the
residential buildings neighboring the project road, sound barrier shall be installed on elevated

4.3.1.2 General Quality of Ambient Air
There are more than 2000 industrial enterprises in Anshan City among which 24 are main
industrial pollution sources according to national standards (The Anshan Iron & Steel
Complex is regarded as one unit ). The systematic emission from these 24 enterprises is up to
168.4 billion m3, which covers 90.3% of systematic industrial emission of the whole city
among which 87.2% comes from Anshan Iron & Steel Complex.
According to monitoring of present situation conducted during EIA. and compared with
GB3095-1996, the percentage of monitoring points beyond standard is shown in Table 4-26.

The concentrations of Point I ( northeast of Anshan Glassworks ) and Point 2 ( Lieshishan St.
residential area ) with project are lower than that of without project. The concentrations of
point 3 ( Tuanjie Primary School ). with and without the project, remains at the same level.
The concentration of Point 4 ( Laodong Road Primary School ) with project is higher than
that of without project. The concentration of Point 5 ( Bajiazi Subdistrict Office) with project
is much lower than that of without project when the dominant Nvind is in south direction and
is lightly higher than that of Nkithout project when the dominant wind is in north direction
because the road shall be changed to the north of the Point afier the implementation of the
project.
North wind makes the concentrations of Point 2 and 3 hig.h. the west wind maximize the
concentration of point 2. and east and south wind maximize the concentration of Point 4 and
5.
The predicted concentrations of CO, HC and NO2 are much lower than the environmental
standard, while the max. Only NOx concentration predicted exceeds the standard. However.
the hourly and daily average concentration of these three pollutants change in the same
pattern at different points and under different wind directions. the CO is therefore selected for
analyzing the impact on environment with and without JRR in 2010. The CO concentration

4.3.4.2 Operational phase
a) Technical Assistance
Anshan City ha: -olemnly promised to develop and implement motor vehicle emission
control strategy (MVECS) to alleviate further worsening of air quality caused by increase of
vehicles and vehicle speed's slow down again in the urban district. The research and
implementation of MVECS of Anshan City is a part of technical assistance (TA) for MVECS
of Liaoning urban transport project. For details, see Annex 3. On the basis of a clear
understanding of issues facing Anshan City, the trends of motor vehicle growth and impact
of the emissions on air quality and knowledge of motor vehicle emission control technologies
and programs, a series of motor vehicle control measures will be developed as the core of the
strategy. These measures will include, but not limited to:
* stringent motor vehicle emission control standards and regulations
*  vehicle inspection and maintenance program
*  catalytic purification facilities
*  engine improvement
* retirement of aged vehicles
*  monitor and enforcing thea motor vehicle emission standards
* promote public transportation
* increase motor vehicle speeds
* motor vehicle quantity control in urban center
* develop clean or alternative fuel technologies
Means of technical assistance include:
* consulting services
* technical workshop
* overseas study and inspection
Working amount of technical assistance
*  local consultants             40 men.months
*  out-of-province consultants   15 men.months
*  workshop                       depending on completion of TOR of TA

4.4 Impact of JRR Project on Surface Water
4.4.1 Assessment Method
ALCOrdingu to milieLu o' eacih roaId secLion of' JRR  pro'ect. the Laodong Bridge section Nwill
influence the surface ri%cr sA item anu Lhe Siouth S.)hahe Ri\er vs ill be directlk at'fected durilln
constructi'.n phase. Otn other r,oald sece'ons. the pollutants x U he bcarried av-ax  y rainfall into
rivcr  c:.Jh ais South Shalhe I'  er. \tirTialnghe Ri         %l via the  municipal sewer network.
Ke%poli it of asse.snicnt is iiinac, ot domestic  >e              0 ace  on  ice  k% i ;tCr. 1rLSil t'l h.
(, '



Liaoning Urban Transport Project-Anshan Subproject       Environmental Impact Assessment
construction team. The impact of JRR project on surface water will be assessed based on
obsernation results of present condition of rivers (South Shahe River etc.) as well as on
draining of waste water during construction phase and of pollutants during operational phase
into rivers. Model of predicting the impact of domestic sewage which is used at site is taken
from JTJ 005-96 "Specifications fio Environment Impacl Assessment of Highway (on trial)".
4.4.2 Impact Analysis
4.4.2.1 Construction Phase
Sewage water during construction phase consists of domestic sewage drained by construction
personnel and a small amount of leakage water from construction facilities. With reference to
construction of similA bridges and condition in Anshan app. 80 workers who will live at site
are estimated to conduct the construction of Laodong Bridge. According to aforementioned
model, 2.31 m3 per day of domestic sewage shall be discharged directly into Nanshahe River.
The sewage from other workers shall be drained into sewer network of the city. According to
measuring statistics provided by Anshan Environmental Monitoring Center in recent years.
daily average of industrial waste water and municipal domestic sewage drained into South
Shahe River amounts up to 340.56 m3/d. Therefore, the domestic sewage from construction
personnel during construction phase has low incremental impact to water quality of South
Shahe River because it is very small in quantity and especially doesn't contain any special
pollutant.
Waste water during construction phase is mainly the oil-bearing sewage produced by
construction equipment because of oil leakage. It is very small in quantity and flows rarely
into rivers. In addition, waste water includes the flushing water for sand and stone, overflow
from agitator of paving material. Since the flushing and agitating will be done not in site and
the flushing water will be reused, this part of waste water has no impact on quality of surface
water.
4.4.2.2 Operational Phase
Due to automobile troubles, traffic accidents and so on. gasoline or machine oil may be
leaked on road surface during operational phase. When it rains, the rainfall will bring all the
oils, dusts and pollutants into rivers via the sewer network.
Table 3-11 (the present status of water quality of South Shahe River) indicates that the water
quality of river at Laodong Bridge section is already far away from class V of the national
surface water standard because of upstream pollution by industrial waste water and domestic
sewage. The pollutants produced by traffic is much smaller in quantity in comparison with
those from industrial waste water and domestic sewage. And after diluted by rainfall the
sewage drainage from JRR project will not affect the water quality of South Shahe River.
The rainfall runoff on the surface of other road sections will be collected in drainage ditches
via the sewer network and finally flow into Yunlianghe River. Amount of pollutants
discharged into rivers will almost be the same before and after JRR project.

4.5.2.1 Construction Phase
The impact on soil and \qt.ctation in constructioni phase descried in this assessment mainlx
refers to the impact on soil and \egetation due tO oCcupaltion of land by road construction.

described in following scction.
In the course of const?uction. the work-site shed and warehouse for building materials will
occupy land. Though the occupation which does not result in change of soil property and in
cutting of trees will not last long at each road section. there shall still be short time change of
land application and short time vegetation damage which can be restored in the future.
4.5.2.2 Analysis of Impact of JRR Project on Soil and Vegetation
On the basis of investigation data of present situation and feasibility study of proposed project,
it can be known from calculation that the project construction will occupy 44350 m2 of farn
land and vegetable plot. This part of land is located at boundary between city and village and
has been divided to land of urban application. That means the owners of land are not living by
it. 15795 m2 of lawn and greenery patches and 6500 m2 of shelter forest and 7130 trees will
be cut down, among which the trees over 25 years account for 60% approximately. Tree
cutting quantity takes app. 70% of alongside trees. In the assessment, according to the size of
tree, approximate calculation of actual greening effect of trees is made, big tree is computed
in terms of 100% of greening area. middle tree 65%. small tree 10% and the newly planted
tree 3.1%. the result of calculation is detailed in Table 4-35.

4.5.3 Mitigation
New trees will be planted on both sides of newly built and widened roads, the spacing
between trees shall be 5 m; flower. grass and shrubbery on the separation belt will be grown.
Because land in city is limited. there are many specific difficulties in raising greening area. In
100



Liaoning Urban Transport Project-Anshan Subproject                   Environmental Impact Assessment
order to reach the greening goal in the near future. the follow ing mitigation measures are put
forward in this environmental assessment specially.
The space between planted trees along the road shall be half of the space (2.5 m) between
adult trees. Several years or over ten years later those trees shall be spaced out or
transplanted.
On the basis of concrete condition of both sides of the road, the climbers, such as virginia
creeper, wild grape and Chinese wisteria etc. can be planted on the available walls of
buildings and piers of interchange etc. These plants can grow upwards, in this way
perpendicular greening will be realized. About 15560 climbers shall be planted, totaling 5187
running meters.
In order to make the environment green, some shade flow-er and plant shall be planted on the
ground under the newly-constructed interchanges.
According to the climate characteristics in this area. poplar and willow shall be chosen as
trees that line a street.
The above mentioned trees shall be planted in the following spring after the road completion.
The construction shall be carried out section by section or side by side, so the raw material for
temporary use can only occupy one or another section or section side of the road to avoid
occupation of land which is not used for this purpose.
By taking the above mitigation measures, after the implementation of this project. the
greening effect of resuming ecology and vegetation is detailed in Table 4-36.

4.6 Sunshine Obstruction Assessment
4.6.1 Methodology
As for Anshan JRR project. there is no elevated road in preferred alignment, and the elevated
road in the alternatives is far away from residential areas. In the design of interchanges and
viaducts, design institute have already paid attention to the problem of sunshine obstruction.
In this assessment, the numerical modeling method will be adopted to evaluate the sunshine
obstruction of JRR project.

4.7 Social Environmental Impact Assessment
4.7.1 Approach and Methodology
Investigation had been made fronm Nov.5th to Dec.'(th to find out the environmental impact
of the proposed project oln roadside environment. Durinig the period. large amount of
information from  subdistrict office. residents committee. industrial and commercials
administration. enterprises and institutions, schools and hospitals etc. had been collected.
particularly. sensitive points along main road sections had beenl investigated. In accordance
with the current situation. traffic \ olume difference in construction and operational phases of
the proposed project, sizes of' to-be-built roads and interchanges and their impacts on
sensitive points along (he road. measures and had also been proposed to alleviate the impact.
4.7.2 Impact Analysis
4.7.2.1 Items impacted in construction phase
* Travelling of pedestrians along both sides of project road.
* Customers and motorless vehicles going in and out of markets
* AISC employees coming and going through the gates.
3  Travelling of vehicles on S-N road and E-W road.
a) Impact on traveling ofpedestriins
Construction of road shall impose short-term impact on traveling of pedestrians along the
both sides of the project road. Impact degree shall be different according to the construction
scale of road sections and the distribution of residents.
(I) In Bailou residential area (section 2-3-2) on the south of Shengli road and the east of
Yongchang Street, the senior citizens over the age of 50 account for 56% of the total
population there (see Table 3-16). Many people go to the People Park on the west side of the
road in the morning and evening. About 100 pupils study in the school on the north side of
the road. construction will affect traveling of over 400 people.
(2) Most residents who live on the east side of Laodong Road (section 3-2-3) shall cross the
road when shopping. Over 200 residents will be affected by the construction.
(3) Changing tramear line at Jianguo Road (section 3-3) to the west will influence about 1 00
residents taking tramcar who live on the east side of the road. They will detour and ride other
buses instead of tramcar.
(4) Many residents who live on the east side and west sides of Yuanlin Road (section 1-3) go
shopping to the market on the east side because the market on the west side is far away from
the residential area. Construction will impose impact on over 200 residents who live on the
west side and go shopping to the east market and less impact on residents live on the east
side.
(5) Residents who live on both sides of Yongchang Street which lies on the west side of
Shengli Road can go shopping on their own side. but usually about 50 residents cross the
street to go shopping and they will suffer impact of construction.
On the west side of north section (3-3) of Jianguo Road there is AISC plant area. The
104



Liaoning Urban Transport Project-Anshan Subproject      Environmental Impact Assessment
residents who live on the east side don't need to cross the road. On the west side of south
section (3-5) of Jianguo Road there are warehouses and shops and is sparsely populated. The
residents living on east side seldom cross the road. South Ring Road and Hebei Road are
newly finished, most residents who lived in the area occupied by the project road have
already moved to other areas before starting of construction, and residual residents can detour
the roads in the village. Thus, construction shall impose less impact on the traveling of the
residents who live in the section mentioned above.
b) Impact on markets and entertainment place
(1) Because both Erdao Street market and Sandao Street market are divided by Yongchang
Street, construction.will impose impact on customers's traveling and thus on business of 12
peddlers on both sides of the road.
A
(2) Every day about 300 handcarts and 500 trucks go to and out of Anshan Fruit Wholesale
Market. Construction shall impose short-term impact on going into and out of the markets of
MV, NMV and customers.
(3) The Old People's Palace is located on the east side of North Jianguo Road and goods
yards and shops are located on the west side, people who go into and out of the Old People's
Palace can detour Qianjin Road or East Minsheng Road.
(4) Since Dongning Market, Decorative Material Market, Vehicles Market, cold storage and
Laodong Road Market etc. are of small size and far away from the project road and they
almost have side gates, people can go to markets via the other roads. Less impact shall be
imposed on NMV and customers going to and out of these markets.
c) Impact on ingoing and outgoing ofAISC employees at some main gates
There are 145000 AISC employees going to and from AISC every day, arnong which 12100
employees ride bicycle. Traffic flow is concentrated on the project road -- at front gate at
North Jianguo Road, Heping gate, Xiaodong gate. Lishan Underpass and Xiaonan gate at
Huangang Road. During the construction, traffic blocks will impose negative influence on
AISC employees going to or going off work.
d) Impacts on schools
(1) About 700, 500, 80, 200 pupils cross the project road to go to NQ 34 Middle School.
Laodong Road primary School, Ng 15 Middle School and Wuyi Road Primary School
respectively. The construction will impose great impact on these schools.
(2) Most pupils can go to Ng 31 Middle School. Gangdu Primary School and Xishahe
Primarv School via other road instead of the project roads. Thus. the construction will impose
little impact on these schools.
(3) Qianjin Primary School is located on the south side of Huangang Road and there is no
residential area on the north side. Qianjin Primary School shall move to the new building on
the south side during construction. Nanchangdian Primarn School is located on the east side
of the project road and there is no residential area oni the wvest side. Thus, the construction1

district government. thus have 'e~N patients. As for a certaiin hospital. 20 patients max. per day
have to cross the street to see a doctor.

a) Outgoing and living quiality of residents duelling along th/Ie road

The widening of Jianguo Rd. and Huangang Rd. will not impose significant impact on the

Changing the line of tramcar will inconvenence the tiamcar riders nearby.
The residents who live on the south side of Yongchang St. and west side of Shengli Rd.
needn't cross the road when shopping, thus the project won't affect the residents as far as
outgoing is concerned.
The reconstruction of Yuanlin Road will impose little impact on resident's outgoing and
crossing the road.
The project has no impact on area neighboring South Ring Rd., because the area is thinly
populated and mainly for industrial use.
The most affected residential area is Bailou Residential (7w) area because 320 teachers,
stu.dents and pupils of Ng 15 Middle School and Gangdu Primary School have to cross the
street and the senior citizens over the age of 50 account for 56% of the total population there.
(2) Impact on living quality
The higher traffic volume and vehicle speed after completioni of the project will lead to
increase in traffic noise, e.g., the noise level in Bailou residential area will increase by 3 dB.
For details of noise impact on residents see Noise Impact Analysis of the report.
For'details of impact of displacement see relevant part in this chapter.

4.7.3 Mitigation
4.7.3.1 Mitigation measures to be taken in constructin phase
Makeshift passage shall be provided for pedestrians crossing the road and going into or out of
the market.
Special personnel shall be provided to be responsible for the security of pupils who have to
cross the construction site.
Low noise equipments shall be preferred. Since most of teaching buildings are far from the
existing road, impact of construction noise on them will not be serious.
The contractor' had better not ca.-rv out the construction in traffic peak hours of non-
motorized vehicles and staff going to and out of work and school hours.
The construction site in Zhanqian area shall be enclosed and the construction shall be carried
out section by section so that the -ehicles can detour through other roads.
The construction of up and down lanes of all proposed road shall be carried out one after
another, such as the widening of south section of Yuanlin Road and the road construction in
front of Fruits Wholesale Market's gate.
The construction of interchanges (or viaducts) near 4 gates of AISC on Jianguo Rd. and of
Minsheng Rd. Interchange (viaduct) shall be carried out in stages. so as to provide gates for
employees and vehicles comingj and going.
The existing underpass (for examinple. the Wuyi Rd. I indcrpass) shall be used for travelinm of
pedestrians and vehicles during the construction ot nc%n interchanges.
The occupants of sensitive buildings to be displaced slhall be compensated by constructioll
units, besides. the newv teaching, bhuildings and residential buildings shall be built prior to the
demolishment of old ones.

Interchanges or viaducts will be built at Lishan Underpass. Wuyi Road Intersection, Heping
Gate and Xiaodong tate etc. to minimize the traffic jams occurring in the peak hours.
c) Set up of three public parking stations
As Anshan City does not possess any standard public parking stations, it is planned to set up
three such stations in front of railway station, near the People Park and at Hunan region where
traffic order is in confusion. The land to be used for this purpose belongs to that of urban
application. These three stations will make contribution to reducing traffic jam, improving
traffic order and giving more safety to pedestrians and vehicles.
d) Set up of big-sized bus station
On the land planned to be used for JRR project, a big-sized bus station shall be set up at the
southeast of Wuyi Road Interchange. At the place, there is no other sensitive point except the
Tengda Disco-theque which will be moved to other place. Wuyi Road Interchange is a hub of
Anshan urban traffic. After completion of reconstruction of Jianguo Road, Huangang Road
aEud Yongchang Road, buses can more easy enter urban area of the city. At the same time,
p%blic traffic vehicles at the big-sized bus station can enter or get out of Jianguo Road
through different lanes of Wuvi Road Interchange. The traffic on Jianguo Road can not be
negatively influenced and the urban traffic of the city shall be accordingly improved.
e) Other traffic facilities
In combination with infrastructure. the JRR project shall provide plant belt for separation at
Jianguo Road, Huangang Road and Yongchang Street and separating railing in the middle of
the road, set up or renew the traffic signal facilities. T-hese measures shall help in improving
the traffic order at city center or commercial tlourishing region, give more safety to
pedestrians crossing street and tIlus raise greatly the living quality of the people.
f) Other mitigation measures
There are some vacant stands in Elrdao Street Market and Sandao Street Market to position
the 12 pedlars whose stands xN ill be occupied by the proposed road.
Greenbelt separation shall he proxided on all the sectionis of road to compensate the loss of
occupied greenery patches.

The construction unit shall compensate the farmers whose land neighboring South Ring Road
and Hebei Road is occupied with respect to stipulations of state policies concerned.

4.7.4 Residual Impact
4.7.4.1 Construction Phase
Impact on main senrsitive points during construction phase is concentrated at influencing
people crossing street-;nd at temporary, unfavourable influence caused by building demolition
due to land acquisition. Sixty percent of such impact can be mitigated through measures
described in EIA report.
4.7.4.2 Operational phase
A series of measures described in EIA report shall be taken to mitigate impact on sensitive
points of ptoject road during the operational phase. The residual impacts are as follows.
a) At intersections of project road and other urban roads of the city, new or renewed signal
facilities to control motor vehicles and manual driving vehicle travelling or pedestrian
walking shall be set up. In addition, port-wise stops of bus and public parking stations shall
be constructed. People crossing streeet can be controlled by signal system of the nearest
intersections. Though a few people have to go 80 m of additional way to get at the nearest
intersection, their walk crossing street shall be safe. and the motor vehicles travelling on lanes
shall be more smooth. The designation of special lanes for public bus and motorless vehicles
shall reduce time needed by people to travel.
b) Residents and students from Bailou residential area shall walk through intersection of
Shengli Road and Yongchang Road. Though a few people have to go 250 m of additional
way, their walking shall become more safe than before.
c) At some intersections to AISC of Jianguo Road and intersection of Minsheng Road.
interchanges, overpassing bridges, signal control systems or designated special lanes for
motorless vehicle shall be provided to separate motor vehicles and motorless vehicles
travelling and solve the problem that vehicles have to make turning. The travelling of
vehicles going in and out of AISC shall become more safe and convenient. More important is
that the problem of traffic confusion and jam at the peak hour when AISC staff go to or go off
work shall be solved. The positive influence is obvious.
d) Motor vehicles, motorless vehicles and the people going in or out of the Fruit Wholesome
Market shall pass through the traffic sentry-box located on Jianguo Road. In addition of
traffic safety, the waiting time of vehicles and pedestrians for passing through shall be
reduced to 2 minutes max.
e) The people on Yongchang Street going in or out of Erdaojie or Sandoajie market shall
walk through the underpass of bridge approach of Wuyi Road Interchange. There shall be no
negative influence on people crossing street. On the contrary. people crossing street shall
112



Liaoning Urban Transport Project-Ansihan Subproject                    Environmental Impact Assessment
become more safe because most vehicles shall travel on the interchange.
